1936.10.30

Unlicensed Japanese Residents in Bingyuan Smuggle and Sell Drugs, Causing Trouble; Japan Raises Serious Protest; Sending Overseas Chinese Out of the Country is Insulting; Increase Troops and Police Under the Pretext of Protection

Japanese Military Claims Negotiations Failed and Will Take Self-Defense Action

(Tianjin) The Hezhong Company case in Bingyuan involved Japanese residents Tanaka Yoshio and Takeda Sueo, who arrived in Bingyuan on the 8th without licenses. They colluded with traitors, rented houses under assumed names, established Hezhong Company, smuggled and sold drugs. Knowing the truth about the situation in the house, they feared being punished and reported it to the authorities. The Jin Court sentenced the lessee to imprisonment and ordered Tanaka to vacate the house, which he refused. Following common practice in Chinese lawsuits, the court sealed the house. Tanaka tore off the seals and protested to the chief of the Kawano Special Service Agency. On the 26th, the Public Security Bureau, fearing public outrage, sent police to protect Hezhong and escorted Takeda out of the country, handing him over to the Japanese Consulate in Zhengzhou. The Japanese side claimed this was an insult and intended to ostracize Japan. Kawano visited Yan again on the night of the 27th, verbally protesting severely, claiming that the lives and property of more than 30 Japanese residents were in danger, and threatened to send military police to protect them. Negotiations are currently underway. (29th Special Dispatch)

(Tianjin) Staff Officer Wachi, at 10:11 AM on the 29th, acting on behalf of Tashiro, visited Consul General Horiuchi to exchange views on the Hezhong Company matter in Taiyuan. He returned to Zhangyuan official residence at noon to report. The Japanese military and the Tianjin Consulate General have decided on a joint approach. Tashiro telegraphed Lieutenant Colonel Kawano, chief of the Taiyuan Special Service Agency, to visit Ge again and lodge a serious verbal protest. The Tianjin Consulate immediately dispatched Police Inspector Shiura with six patrol officers to Bingyuan to protect Japanese residents. The Japanese military declared that if negotiations did not yield satisfactory results, they would take self-defense measures and resolutely deal with the situation. The issue of establishing a consulate in Taiyuan, as it is not a treaty port, was proposed by the Japanese side this spring, but Yan did not approve. However, the Tianjin Consulate General has long sought to expand its consular police authority in that area but had no opportunity. A month ago, it dispatched Uetsuma, an officer from the police station, and Nakayama, a translator, to reside locally to prepare for the establishment of a police sub-station and consulate, secretly immigrating people to that area, under the pretext of protecting overseas Chinese and setting up a police presence. Recently, the Hezhong Company incident occurred, and the Suiyuan situation is about to erupt again. The military intends to restrain Yan from looking north and, in cooperation with the consulate, is making a mountain out of a molehill with this case. Wachi plans to fly to Bingyuan within days to convey the military's intentions to Kawano. (29th Special Dispatch)

Japanese Planes Conduct Reconnaissance over Baoding, and Also Over Taiyuan and Baotou

(Baoding) A small Japanese single-wing reconnaissance plane flew from the southwest over Baoding's airspace at low altitude for a week at 8:00 AM on the 29th, then flew northeast. (29th Central News Agency Dispatch)

(Beiping) Two Japanese planes flew to Taiyuan and Baotou this morning. One plane that went to Bingyuan flew back to Ping in the afternoon. (29th Special Dispatch)

Tensions Re-emerge in Eastern Suiyuan; Wang Ying's Bandit Troops Transferred to the Rear; One Side Does Not Abandon Attempt to Invade

(Beiping) A person from Eastern Suiyuan said that there was a mutiny among Wang Ying's bandit troops stationed near Shangdu. Li Shouxin discovered this and transferred them to the rear. Currently, one side has not abandoned its attempt to invade Eastern Suiyuan and has ordered Li Shouxin and Li Jinjia to serve as vanguards, planning to invade Eastern Suiyuan. Recently, the situation on the border of Eastern Suiyuan has become tense again. (29th Special Dispatch)

(Zhangjiakou) According to Shangdu news, the new plan for the puppet bandits to invade the west has been rescheduled to be completed by the end of the year. Wang Ying's and Li Shouxin's units are the main force. Wang's unit will attack Taolin from Shangdu, with the supply station and support team located in Shangdu and Jiabusi. Li's unit will scout Xinghe from Nanhouchang and Daqinggou, west of Zhangbei, with the supply station and support team stationed in Zhangbei. Currently, the puppet bandit units in Chahar Province are extremely busy transporting military supplies. Heavy-duty trucks and camels are constantly on the road. Because someone interceded on Wang Ying's behalf, he has been allowed to reorganize his old troops. (29th Special Dispatch)

British and American Oil Merchants Request Strict Anti-Smuggling Measures

(Tianjin) There is a large amount of smuggled kerosene being hoarded in Tianjin. Every night, it is transported to the suburbs of Tianjin by bicycle, and then transferred to nearby towns for dumping sales. British and American oil merchants are affected. On the 29th, they sent representatives to visit the Tianjin Customs Commissioner, requesting strict anti-smuggling measures. (29th Dispatch)

Japanese Newspaper Discusses Anglo-Japanese Cooperation; Japan Believes There is No Need to Adjust Relations Between the Two Countries; Has Prepared to Abandon the Concept of Cooperation with Britain

(Tokyo) According to the Kokumin Shimbun, after careful study, the Japanese diplomatic authorities have made a final judgment on the Anglo-Japanese cooperation issue, namely, that Japan has no need to actively engage in adjusting Anglo-Japanese relations. The newspaper recalls that this issue was repeatedly raised around April of this year when Japanese Ambassador to Britain Yoshida went to London to take office. The favorable atmosphere that existed among intellectuals and governments of the two countries has had no opportunity to materialize due to the Japanese government's determination to adopt a policy of non-interference in China by other countries. The newspaper also claims that Britain has blocked the import of Japanese goods into its territory. In terms of trade, the situation between the two countries is tantamount to a state of war. However, Britain still demands that Japan provide adequate guarantees for its interests in China. Leaders of the Japanese government now realize the unfairness of this situation and are prepared to abandon the concept of cooperation with Britain. The Japanese naval authorities have also stated that even after the naval treaty is abolished, the Japanese navy will be fully capable of defending the country with its own strength. (29th Reuters Dispatch)

Chinese and Japanese Diplomats Did Not Meet Yesterday

(Nanjing) Regarding the meeting between Zhang Qun and Kawagoe, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs says that no appointment has been made. The diplomatic personnel of both sides did not meet on the 29th. Matsumura, the third secretary of the Japanese Embassy, visited the Director of the International Affairs Department of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs at 10:00 AM on the 29th. It was to discuss general matters and had nothing to do with Sino-Japanese negotiations. (29th Special Dispatch)

Grain Prices Soar in Peiping; One Side Entrusts Grain Merchants to Buy Up Supplies

(Beiping) Grain prices are soaring in Peiping, and the authorities are trying to suppress them. The reason is that many grain merchants in areas such as Caiyu (town name) in southern Peiping are entrusted by one side to buy up as much miscellaneous grain as possible. Dozens of trucks are transported to Langfang every day. It is rumored that people from Zhangjiakou are also buying a lot. (29th Central Dispatch)

(Beiping) Several large merchants have arrived in Caiyu Town, south of Peiping, in recent days to purchase various grains for one side. Dozens of trucks are transported to Langfang every day. (29th Special Dispatch)

(Jinan) Grain prices in this province are still soaring. The Provincial Relief Association is preparing winter relief, and the municipal government is planning to set up large-scale shelters to provide relief to the poor. (29th Special Dispatch) (Nanchang) Rice prices have risen from five yuan to eight yuan. The rural economy has improved, and the sales of native cloth are booming. Gan rice is being sold to Guangdong through official and commercial transport companies. (29th Special Dispatch)

(Taiyuan) After the official proposed price stabilization measures, grain prices have stabilized slightly and are showing a downward trend. (29th Special Dispatch)

Japanese Textile Industry Prepares to Establish Factories in Tianjin

(Tianjin) Osaka Kishiwada Textile Co., Fuji Textile Co., and Donghua Textile Co., all Japanese spinning companies, have sent personnel to North China to investigate and prepare to establish factories in Tianjin. Currently, there are already nine Japanese yarn factories investing in Tianjin. (29th Special Dispatch)

Japan's Trade with China Increases; Willing to Grant Us Short-Term Credit Loans; Abandoning Laissez-faire Policy and Implementing Appropriate Control

(Tokyo) Although Sino-Japanese negotiations are currently extremely tense, it is surprising that Japan's export trade to China has not only not decreased but has greatly increased. It is reported that China has recently placed a large number of orders with enterprises operated by major Japanese conglomerates, such as the South Manchuria Railway Company, Mitsubishi, Mitsui, and Nisshin. Even small and medium-sized industrial and commercial companies are overwhelmed with orders. In all aspects of the Japanese business world, activity seems to be greatly increased due to Chinese demand. It is generally believed here that the increase in the purchasing power of Chinese farmers is due to this year's bumper harvest, which has had a positive impact on the urban economy. Another important reason is the increasing demand for goods from the Chinese people, and the implementation of China's economic construction plans requires huge quantities of raw materials, some of which are supplied by Japan at low prices. The diplomatic authorities here are paying close attention to the above situation and are planning to increase economic relations with China to maintain the status quo for as long as possible. It is reported that the Japanese diplomatic authorities have prepared the following measures: (1) The Japanese government will use the British method as a blueprint and guarantee short-term credit loans to China for goods that are closely related to Japan's economic policy towards China. (2) Develop the organization of Sino-Japanese trade associations in Shanghai, Tianjin, Osaka, and other places. Prime Minister Hirota already had this plan when he was Minister of Foreign Affairs. (3) If China reduces tariffs on Japanese goods, Japan is also willing to consider reciprocal tariff issues. (4) Japan is prepared to adjust the so-called special trade in eastern Hebei within a considerable scope. (5) Regarding Japan's trade with China, implement appropriate control and abandon the laissez-faire policy that has been adopted in the past. (29th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Zhang Zizhong Hosts Farewell Banquet for British Military Commander

(Tianjin) Zhang Zizhong returned to Tianjin from Peiping on the 29th and hosted a farewell banquet for British military commander Burleigh in the evening. (29th Special Dispatch)

(Beiping) Zhang Zizhong came to Peiping to meet with Song, but he left Peiping to return to Tianjin due to important official business. (29th Special Dispatch)

National Government Issues Decree to Honor Yang Yongtai; He Chengjun and Others Request Hubei Provincial Government to Allocate Funeral Expenses; Yang's Coffin is Scheduled to be Moved to Wuchang on the Second of Next Month

(Nanjing) The National Government recently announced a decree to honor Yang Yongtai as follows: Yang Yongtai, member and chairman of the Hubei Provincial Government, had broad knowledge and loyal intentions. In recent years, he assisted in suppressing bandits and spared no effort. Recently, he presided over the Hubei provincial government, planning diligently and achieving remarkable achievements. He was expected to further expand his grand plans and be relied upon for a long time. It was shocking to hear of his assassination and death, and there is deep mourning. Yang Yongtai should be given preferential treatment from the competent authorities and given funeral expenses of 10,000 yuan. His life deeds should be recorded and sent to the historical museum to highlight his loyalty. This decree. (29th Special Dispatch)

(Hankou) He Chengjun and others are all advocating for a grand funeral for Yang Yongtai. In addition to the 10,000 yuan allocated by the central government, they also request the provincial government to allocate 30,000 yuan for funeral expenses to show respect for virtue and reward meritorious service. Yang's coffin is scheduled to be moved to Wuchang on the 2nd. (29th Special Dispatch)

(Hankou) Meng Guangpeng, director of the Department of Civil Affairs, has just resigned from his concurrent position as acting chairman. Liu Zhenhua and He Cheng jointly telegraphed Chiang, requesting that Lu Zhu be replaced. Currently, provincial government affairs are still handled by Lu as an agent before receiving Chiang's explicit orders. (29th Special Dispatch)

Page 4

He Jian and Liu Jianxu Arrive in Nanjing by Air to Participate in Chiang's Birthday Commemoration Ceremony; Chiang Has Already Written a Speech

(Nanjing) Hunan Provincial Chairman He Jian, together with Fourth Route Army Commander Liu Jianxu and ten entourage members, arrived in Nanjing by China Aviation plane at 5:00 PM on the 29th. He and Liu came to wish Chairman Chiang a happy birthday. After participating in the birthday commemoration ceremony held in Nanjing on the 31st, they will return to Hunan. (29th Special Dispatch)

(Hankou) He Jian, Liu Jianxu, and others arrived in Hubei by car from Hunan on the 29th to mourn Yang and visit He. They flew to Nanjing at noon to participate in the aircraft presentation and birthday celebration ceremony before returning to Hunan. (29th Special Dispatch)

(Nanjing) On the 31st, Chairman Chiang Kai-shek's 50th birthday, a grand aircraft presentation and birthday celebration ceremony will be held in the capital. The whole country will hang flags to celebrate, to show respect for the leader. Chiang himself is deeply moved by the enthusiastic collection of funds by the people of the whole country to purchase aircraft and has written a speech, which will be disclosed on the 31st. The full text, about 4,000 words, expresses his concern for the country and his thoughts of his parents, sincerity and earnestness, expressing encouragement and gratitude for the enthusiasm of the people in donating money to purchase aircraft, and expressing deep affection and expectations for the youth during the schooling period, hoping that the people of the country will strive to become stronger and fulfill their national duties. (29th Special Dispatch)

Broadcasting Celebrations for Chairman Chiang Kai-shek's Birthday; De Wang Sends a Telegram to Congratulate Chiang on His Birthday

(Nanjing) The Central Broadcasting Station has specially arranged a celebration program on the 31st for Chairman Chiang Kai-shek's 50th birthday, divided into (1) for European friendly people and overseas Chinese, (2) for domestic audiences, (3) for American friendly people and overseas Chinese, (4) for domestic audiences, and (5) for domestic audiences, foreigners, and Nanyang overseas Chinese. The broadcasting time for each item is from 5:00 AM to 11:30 PM, and the broadcast programs are in Mandarin, Cantonese, and English. (29th Central News Agency Dispatch)

(Nanjing) De Wang originally planned to come to Nanjing to celebrate President Chiang's 50th birthday, but he was unable to spare the time due to the complicated political affairs of the Mengjiang Government. He sent a telegram to congratulate, praising President Chiang's merits in the party and the country, and prepared several valuable birthday gifts, sending personnel to Nanjing to show his celebration and admiration. (29th Central News Agency Dispatch)

(Hankou) Bishop Xi of Hankou, Bishop Ai of Wuchang, and Bishop Gao of Hanyang jointly notified all Catholic believers in Wuhan to hold Mass to celebrate Chiang's birthday and pray for the country in their respective Catholic churches on the 31st. (29th Central News Agency Dispatch)

(Hangzhou) The Zhejiang Provincial Party Headquarters telegraphed a prayer to Vice Chairman Chiang Kai-shek on the 29th, saying, "Auspicious times are beginning, and a famous person is born into the world. Having been entrusted with great responsibility, he must have a long life. In this happy autumn of peace and unity, we celebrate the 50th anniversary of his birth. The whole world is rejoicing, celebrating Mount Gang and Mount Ling. We wish for his boundless blessings and offer the blessings of Huafeng." (29th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Jiangsu Province's Aircraft Presentation Ceremony

(Zhenjiang) Jiangsu Province's Aircraft Presentation Birthday Celebration Ceremony was held at Jurong Airport on the 29th. More than 1,000 representatives from all walks of life and more than 10,000 people from participating groups and the general public attended. Chen Guofu presided over the meeting, reporting that the aircraft presentation to celebrate Chiang's birthday was to increase the country's strength. Then, Ms. Zhou Min cut the ribbon, and nine aircraft took off in formation for a performance. The audience cheered thunderously, and the atmosphere was warm and tense. After the nine aircraft performed, they flew over Zhenjiang and circled several times before returning to Nanjing. They will fly around the province at a later date. Wang Bailing, the chief representative of Jiangsu's aircraft presentation, and ten representatives from all walks of life will go to Nanjing at noon on the 30th and present the aircraft on the morning of the 31st. (29th Special Dispatch)

(Nanchang) The Jiangxi government, military, business, and academic circles held a naming ceremony for four aircraft at the old airport at 9:00 AM today. More than 10,000 people from all walks of life attended in formation. A celebration meeting is scheduled to be held on the 31st, with a review of citizen corps, boy scouts, and service groups, and a lantern parade in the evening. (29th Special Dispatch)

(Hangzhou) Six aircraft from Zhejiang No. 1 to Zhejiang No. 6, along with ten aircraft from Shanghai and ten aircraft from Jiangsu, were flown from Hangzhou to Nanjing by Gao Zhihang, dispatched by the Aviation School at 8:00 AM this morning, to participate in Chiang's birthday aircraft presentation ceremony on the 31st. (29th Special Dispatch)

(Shantou) Shantou has collected more than 10,000 yuan for aircraft purchases. Many parties have not yet reported or announced their donations. (29th Special Dispatch)

(Hong Kong) Donations for aircraft purchases in Guangzhou reached more than 600,000 yuan as of the 29th, and are expected to reach one million. (29th Special Dispatch)

(Nanjing) The Jianyuan Co., Ltd., composed of overseas Chinese from Nanyang, donated 100,000 yuan for Chiang's 50th birthday to the aircraft purchase commemorative committee of all circles in the country, which was very enthusiastic, and requested the purchase of an aircraft named Jianyuan to express their congratulations. The association resolved to invite Huang Jiangquan, general manager of the company, as one of the presidiums at the fourth regular meeting on the 28th. (29th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Junior High School Students Donate Money to Buy Aircraft

(Nanjing) Hong Wenyuan, a first-year student at Jinling Middle School, donated 100 yuan from his savings to the Nanjing Social Affairs Bureau to be forwarded to the Capital's Aircraft Purchase Birthday Celebration Committee for aircraft purchase donations. (29th Special Dispatch)

Prince A Heads South

(Beiping) Prince A left Peiping for Nanjing this morning. According to reports, he met with Song yesterday, and the talks were very satisfactory. This trip to Nanjing is to represent the Suiyuan-Mongolia Association to wish Chiang a happy birthday and to visit Chairman Lin and the central authorities to report on Mongolian affairs. Because the communist bandits in the northwest recently fled to Ningxia and are very rampant, the defense of the adjacent Ikh Juu League is extremely important. The Suiyuan-Mongolia Association urgently hopes that the central government will quell the remaining bandits as soon as possible to prevent them from fleeing east and spreading harm to the local area. After finishing business in Nanjing, he will return north. (29th Special Dispatch)

(Jinan) Today, Prince A is passing through Jinan to go to Nanjing. Two thousand communist bandits are on the border between Ikh Juu League and Ningxia, planning to flee east. The banner army is weak, and it has been decided to visit Chiang to request assistance. (29th Special Dispatch)

Situation of Japanese Military Exercises in Peiping and Tianjin; Yesterday Was a Counter-Offensive Operation by the First and Second Regiments; Imagining Red and White Armies Competing for Peiping and Tianjin

(Tianjin) On the 29th, the Japanese military's first and second regiments in Peiping and Tianjin conducted a counter-offensive exercise, following the operational plan of the military headquarters. The first regiment, the White Army, was the main attacking force, and the second regiment, the Red Army, was the main defending force. The strategic assumption was that after the White Army captured Tianjin, it pursued the remaining enemy forces in Beicang and Yangcun and searched Tianjin. On the morning of the 29th, they continued to attack Beiping and fought fiercely with the enemy in Fengtai, Lugouqiao, and Tongzhou. The Red Army, with Mutaguchi as the commander-in-chief, set up its headquarters in Fengtai, serving as the main defending force. The Kanda Detachment and the Suzuki Artillery Regiment were on the left and right wings of Tongzhou and Dugouqiao. The White Army, with Kayashima as the commander-in-chief, set up its rear defense headquarters at An'ding Station, in charge of the frontal attack. The Kagawa and Nakajima detachments were responsible for taking the two sides of Tongzhou and Lugouqiao. It was assumed that the Red Army's rear defense tracks were destroyed, communication was cut off, and they were forced to retreat to the left bank of the Lugouqiao Yongding River. On the morning of the 31st, the White Army gained the strength of engineers to build bridges and rafts, and forcibly crossed the river, defeating the Red Army. The army rested on the 1st and continued to attack Beiping on the 2nd. (29th Special Dispatch)

(Tianjin) On the morning of the 29th, five special trains departed from Tianjin to An'ding on the Peiping-Tianjin line, transporting Japanese infantry, artillery, and cavalry, preparing for the major exercise to begin on the morning of the 30th. The first train left at 1:00 AM, carrying 700 infantry, 50 horses, and 6 heavy artillery pieces. The second train left at 1:30 AM, carrying 70 cavalry and 140 horses. The third train left at 3:00 AM, carrying 160 artillerymen and 5 armored vehicles. The fourth train left at 3:30 AM, carrying 70 artillerymen, 6 field guns, and 16 heavy trucks. The fifth train, attached to the Peiping-Shenyang train, carried 120 cavalry from Tanggu and Zhanhua, 800 infantry from Tianjin, and 4 artillery pieces. All five trains arrived at An'ding and disembarked. Kayashima, commander of the Second Infantry Regiment, Tomobe, commander of the Tangshan Detachment, Kagawa, commander of the Tanggu Detachment, and Nakajima, commander of the Yuguan Detachment, all went to An'ding on the fifth train to arrange military affairs. (29th)

(Beiping) According to a phone call from Fengtai, more than 850 Japanese soldiers camping in Fengtai are resting today and have not gone out for exercises all day. It is scheduled to gather at the Japanese barracks at around 3:00 AM on the 30th. At 5:00 AM, all more than 800 Japanese soldiers will take machine guns, steel cannons, and war horses on foot to An'ding on the Peiping-Ning Line to resist the Japanese army in Tianjin. (29th Special Dispatch)

(Beiping) According to people from the four suburbs, since the Japanese military exercises, they have occupied more than a dozen villages and houses in the eastern and southern suburbs, taking peasants' miscellaneous grains to feed the horses. They may pay for it in the future. Residents, because they have not seen this before, are mostly suspicious and fearful, and have moved to Peiping to live. (29th Special Dispatch)

Chairman Chiang Kai-shek Arrives in Luoyang

(Luoyang) Chairman Chiang Kai-shek arrived in Luoyang, accompanied by Qian Dajun, director of the First Office of the Attendant Room. Qian Zongze, director of the Longhai Railway Bureau, also arrived in Luoyang. Chiang wore a yellow military uniform, his spirit was vigorous, his bearing was extraordinary, and his steps were very strong. After getting off the train, he went to the military school to rest. (29th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Central Standing Committee Meeting

(Nanjing) The Central Committee held the 24th Standing Committee meeting at 9:00 AM on the 29th. More than 20 committee members, including Ye Chucang, Ding Weifen, Feng Yuxiang, Lin Sen, Zhang Ji, Fang Zhi, Zhou Qigang, Zhang Lisheng, and Shao Yuanchong, attended. They discussed many routine cases and decided to hold a memorial week next Monday, and first hold a memorial service for the death of martyr Huang Xing. Committee member Zhang Ji was assigned to attend the report. The meeting adjourned at about 10 o'clock. (29th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Restoration Commemoration Held in Taiyuan

(Taiyuan) Bingyuan held a commemoration of the Xinhai Revolution today. Yan Xishan, Zhao Daiwen, Fu Zuoyi, Xu Yongchang, and other civil and military officials led a ceremony at the Zhaoyi Temple to pay tribute to the martyrs, and then went to the Da Jiao field to review the anti-communist defense corps and civil servants, etc. More than 10,000 people participated, which was extremely enthusiastic. Yan said that we should step on the blood and move forward to complete national independence and autonomy. During the meeting, a Japanese plane flew around the sky over Bingyuan for several weeks, seemingly for reconnaissance purposes. (29th Special Dispatch)

British Ambassador Hosts a Banquet for Our Officials

(Nanjing) British Ambassador Sir Hughe Knatchbull-Hugessen hosted a banquet at the embassy at 8:00 PM on the 29th to entertain our country's officials and celebrate. More than ten people, including Foreign Minister Zhang, attended. Everyone enjoyed themselves until about 9 o'clock. (29th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Personnel from the Chief Inspectorate Head North

(Nanjing) The first batch of personnel from the Anti-Smuggling Inspectorate of Road Transport took the Jinpu train north on the 29th. The remaining personnel are led by Deputy Director Li Tonghua and will continue on the 30th. The office is scheduled to start working in Tianjin on November 2nd. Also, Ansell, the Director-General of the office, went to Shanghai on the 29th. After visiting the Inspector General of Customs for instructions, he will go to Tianjin from Shanghai. (29th Central Dispatch)

Ministry of Finance Discusses Food Issues

(Nanjing) Gao Bingfang, Director of the Tax Department of the Ministry of Finance, invited representatives from various departments in the Ministry of Interior and the Economic Commission, Xu Tinghu and Wen Juntian, to the ministry on the 29th to discuss the special tax issue in the financial revenue and expenditure system law. Regarding the adjustment of food surpluses and deficits and the equalization of food prices, he consulted the opinions of the representatives of various ministries and commissions responsible for agriculture, land administration, or people's livelihood. It is planned to formally invite responsible personnel from various ministries and commissions in charge of agriculture, land administration, or people's food to hold another meeting to discuss fundamental measures for controlling food. (29th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Ministry of Finance Plans to Unify the Currency System

(Nanjing) In order to unify the currency system, the Ministry of Finance is preparing to restore the mints in Wuchang, Xi'an, and Chongqing. It is organizing and repairing the existing usable machinery and specializing in casting copper-nickel subsidiary coins. It has dispatched Hu Yong and Xie Guangyu to inspect. After completion, it will prepare a plan and submit it to Confucius for approval. (29th Special Dispatch)

The Executive Yuan Cares About the Nanning Flood; Allocates 100,000 Yuan for Relief

(Nanjing) After the Executive Yuan received a report from the Guangxi Provincial Government on the flood situation in the Nanning area, it decided to allocate 100,000 yuan from the National Government for relief. Li Rongkai, secretary of the Ministry of Finance, and inspector Cao Zhonggui will go to Guizhou to survey and distribute the funds together with the Guizhou Provincial Government. Li and Cao are scheduled to take the night train to Shanghai on the 29th and visit Minister Kong for instructions before taking a boat around Hong Kong to Guizhou. (29th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Chiang Tingfu Telegraphed Passing Through Vladivostok

(Nanjing) Chiang Tingfu, our ambassador to the Soviet Union, telegraphed the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, reporting that he arrived in Vladivostok on the morning of the 29th and took a special train attached to the express train to Moscow to take office. He is expected to arrive around the 8th of next month. (29th Special Dispatch)

Child Laborers and Apprentices are Prohibited from Carrying Heavy Loads; Chiang's Handwritten Order to the Beijing Municipal Government

(Nanjing) Chairman Chiang Kai-shek handwrote an order to the Beijing Municipal Government stating that child laborers and apprentices who are underage should be prohibited from carrying heavy loads. Their household registration should be investigated and punished. Those who do not sit properly in cars, those who do not button their clothes, and those who walk crookedly should be strictly interfered with and corrected by the police and patrolling inspectors. (29th Special Dispatch)

American Newspaper Criticizes Japanese Military Exercises: Seemingly Military Actions with a Definite Purpose, Clearly Intending to Force China to Accept Their Demands

(Washington) The Washington Post commented today on the Japanese military's exercises in Pingjin, saying that these Japanese exercises, with their broad scope and large number of participating troops, give the impression that this is not an exercise but a military action with a definite purpose. This is nothing more than Japan clearly intending to force the Chinese government to accept its demands regarding North China. This kind of exercise is merely a demonstration that if Japan's demands are rejected, its military will take action. However, the Chinese authorities absolutely cannot endlessly comply with Japan, because Chinese public opinion unanimously recognizes Japan's insatiable greed and insists that no further concessions should be made. (28th National Telegram)

Guangdong Courts: Determined to Thoroughly Rectify

(Hong Kong) After inspecting the various courts and prisons in Guangdong, Wang Yongbin believes they are corrupt and dark and has decided to thoroughly rectify them. (29th Special Telegram)

Outside Lushun Waters: Smuggling Ship Sunk by Collision

(Tianjin) The Japanese smuggling ship "Kinmaru," loaded with smuggled goods, was sailing from Lushun to the Luan River estuary when it was struck and sunk by the Norwegian cargo ship "So-and-So" fifteen nautical miles outside Lushun. The Japanese captain and six crew members fell into the sea and were rescued by the Norwegian ship, delivered to Tanggu on the morning of the 29th. (29th Special Telegram)

American Embassy: Hunting Scheduled for Next Month

(Beiping) Officers and soldiers of the US Embassy Guard and Marine Corps stationed in China are scheduled to hunt in the area near Lugouqiao successively from the 3rd of next month until December 31st. The relevant Chinese authorities have been notified, and local military police will be instructed to provide protection at that time. (29th Special Telegram)

Tianjin Political Prisoners Resume Eating

(Tianjin) The hunger strike of political prisoners in the Third Prison has ended. The prison authorities have granted their requests, and the prisoners resumed eating on the 29th. (29th Special Telegram)

Overseas Chinese Laborers: Ministry of Industries Handles Registration

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Industries is handling the registration of overseas Chinese laborers. From May to July of this year, over 13,000 people have already been registered. (19th Special Telegram)

Guizhou Provincial Government: Requests Subsidy for Government Expenses

(Nanjing) The Guizhou Provincial Government telegraphed the Executive Yuan, stating that the Guizhou provincial goods tax is similar to the likin tax, and they now intend to abolish it. However, the provincial treasury's expenditures are insufficient, so they request that the central government allocate a special fund to subsidize government expenses by 100,000 yuan per month to make up for the shortfall. The Yuan has submitted this to the Ministry of Finance for review. (29th Special Telegram)

Zhou Zuomin Arrives in Nanjing

Japanese and Puppet Troops' "Autumn Suppression" Anti-Japanese Army's Counter-Battle News Well-Informed, Tactics Clever, Sanjiang Area Most Powerful, Future Bitter Half Year

Harbin Dispatch, Since entering the summer, the Northeast Anti-Japanese Volunteer Army has begun to be very active due to the growth of sorghum. Because the Japanese and puppet troops were afraid of suffering heavy sacrifices, they did not dare to attack, but could only listen to it. Since entering autumn, the sorghum has been harvested by farmers for the most part. The Japanese army believes that this is the best time to attack the Anti-Japanese Army and implement its so-called "Autumn Bandit Suppression" plan. The details of each situation are as follows:

Transfer and Transportation in Northeast China

The transfer and transportation of Japanese and puppet troops in Northeast China for the attack on the Anti-Japanese Volunteer Army was completed in mid-September. From October 1st, they began to attack the Anti-Japanese Volunteer Army. Since then, the Anti-Japanese Army has fought against the Japanese and puppet troops in this difficult environment until the end of March next year, actually including the three seasons of autumn (October and November), winter (December and January), and spring (February and March). Recently, the climate in Northeast China has been severely cold. The Anti-Japanese Army, running on the mountains and forests, is inadequately clothed and fed, and the wind and snow are tearing at their skin. The iron weapons held in their hands are as cold as ice, permeating their hearts. In the snow-covered mountains and under the moonlight, they are working hard to fight for the love of their motherland. Their heroic passion contains the legacy of ancient warriors. As for their willingness to endure danger and hardship, it is even more unknown to outsiders.

Sanjiang Anti-Japanese Army

The military focus of this "Autumn Bandit Suppression" by the Japanese and puppet troops is the pseudo-Sanjiang Province and the pseudo-Binjiang Province in the Fourth Military Region. The Anti-Japanese Volunteer Army in Northeast China, except for the pseudo-Andong Province and the Eastern Border Region of the pseudo-Fengtian Province in the pseudo-First Military Region, which still have active Anti-Japanese Volunteer Army, the one that makes the Japanese and puppet troops most worried is the Anti-Japanese Volunteer Army in the pseudo-Sanjiang Province, because its momentum is the greatest, and there are mountains stretching across several counties. They occupy the mountains and defend the danger, and there is a sense of one husband being in charge, and ten thousand troops being unable to attack. According to the information, the Anti-Japanese Volunteer Army in the pseudo-Sanjiang Province region includes Xia Yunjie, Zhao Shangzhi, Dai Hongbin, Li Huatang, Xie Wendong, Wang Zibin, Tian Yuan, Yan Wang, Mingshan, Wang Yinwu, Tian Yi, Dongshanhui, Da Yimian, Zouzi, Zhanshanhao, Haihong, Yunzhonghao, Li Sihai, Wang Sihai, and various troops numbering more than 20,000 people in Luobei, Huachuan, Tangyuan, and Yilan in the north and south mountains of the Songhua River. Other famous Anti-Japanese Army leaders in Raohe, Baoqing, Boli, and other places include Cui Yishan, Li Xuefang, Lord Mengchang, Commander Guan, etc. Most of them are organized, use new tactics and new weapons in their combat methods, and have fairly detailed marching plans. They also have a political propaganda department, and their goal of propaganda to the people is to save the motherland and drive the enemies out of Northeast China. The Japanese and puppet troops feel very棘手about this kind of Anti-Japanese Volunteer Army with political colors.

Avoid Strength and Attack Weakness

The tactics adopted by the various Anti-Japanese Volunteer Army in the pseudo-Sanjiang Province region are mostly "avoiding strength and attacking weakness" in order to avoid suffering heavy sacrifices. Therefore, the various Anti-Japanese Volunteer Army are densely deployed with scouts everywhere, and the news is extremely well-informed. They rarely clash head-on with the Japanese and puppet troops. Sometimes the Anti-Japanese Volunteer Army uses the tactic of luring the enemy deep, and the Japanese and puppet troops often suffer heavy losses. According to reliable news, the Anti-Japanese Volunteer Army has more than 50 light machine guns and more than 20 mortars, but the clothing is very mixed and uneven. Sometimes a small team is found wearing Japanese military uniforms and copper helmets. When the Japanese and puppet troops see them, they cannot distinguish between true and false, and they are suddenly shot, which makes the attacking Japanese and puppet troops feel the difficulty of combat.

Leader Experience

Among the leaders of the Anti-Japanese Volunteer Army, such as Zhao Shangzhi, who graduated from the Six Schools in Beiping, is clear-headed and has considerable wisdom, while Xia Yunjie is an extremely stubborn and rude Han Chinese who does not wash his face all year round. He once vowed to his subordinates that he would not wash his face until the day of success. Seeing his short stature, he has such a magical and firm idea. The Japanese and puppet troops are most afraid of these Anti-Japanese Army leaders and troops.

Japanese and Puppet Troop Situation

The Japanese and puppet troops in this "Autumn Bandit Suppression" in the Sanjiang Province region, in addition to the original troops, also transferred a certain brigade stationed in the Qiqihar area of the pseudo-Third Military Region and a large number of Japanese and puppet troops from various sources to come here to reinforce. Because their secrecy is not known to anyone, it is very difficult to know how many troops there are. They have recently begun to fight fiercely with the Anti-Japanese Volunteer Army and will continue for six months. The training of these Japanese and puppet troops is presided over by Okada, a Japanese advisor in the pseudo-Sanjiang Province region. They often conduct exercises. After sending the well-trained Japanese and puppet troops to the war zone, they conduct a second batch of training. As for the soil killed by the Anti-Japanese Volunteer Army, they build loyalty spirit pagodas to commemorate them in order to encourage those who come to die later. Before the battle, they instill the so-called "loyalty to the emperor and defense of the country" into the soldiers to encourage them.

An Analysis of China's Recent Finances (Part 1)

-- Sun Huairen

Since the implementation of the currency system reform on November 4th of last year, the authorities then issued a declaration saying that after the new currency system was implemented for 18 months, China's fiscal revenue and expenditure could be balanced. The issuance of this statement clearly shows that the implementation of the new currency system is inextricably linked to the central government's finances. Therefore, people who are concerned about financial issues must not only pay attention to the changes in the financial situation itself, but also pay close attention to the dynamics of the new currency system. Here, if we take that authority's declaration as a logical major premise, then, if the new currency system is not implemented, of course China's finances cannot be balanced after 18 months, or if it is implemented and fails, China's finances cannot be balanced after 18 months either. Whether this inference is wrong depends on whether the major premise is wrong. On the other hand, since the new currency system and China's central government finances have such a close relationship, of course the situation of finances itself is also sufficient to affect the effect of the new currency system.

Thus, two major opposing psychologies have also arisen in people's observation of China's economic future. The first type of people highly value the new currency system, believing that after the new currency system is implemented, China's trade, China's purchasing power, and everything in China's economy will tend to be prosperous, and fiscal revenue and expenditure will naturally be balanced. This type of people can be given a name and called the "optimistic faction of the new currency system." The second type of people, on the contrary, attach importance to the unsoundness of China's finances, believing that before improving the current financial essence, revenue and expenditure cannot be balanced, and that what the new currency system can do to balance finances only lies in the possibility of inflation. Therefore, this faction is the "pessimistic faction of the new currency system." Those who are optimistic about the new currency system are obviously also optimistic about China's finances; similarly, those who are pessimistic about the new currency system are of course also pessimistic about China's finances.

It has been almost twelve months since the currency reform, and there is only half a year left before the 18-month deadline in the declaration. In the past two-thirds of the appointment period, although we have not seen inflation on the surface, we have not seen any obvious improvement in the central government's finances either. On September 6th, Finance Minister Kong once talked to reporters about the recent situation of the central government's finances. It is said that the fiscal deficit in the past year reached 200 million yuan. Fortunately, we adhered to the principle of increasing revenue and reducing expenditure, and made every effort to maintain it, and reorganized tax collection and saved various expenses, so that we could safely get through the difficulties. In the current year, with the unification of Guangdong and Guangxi, the national credit has become more consolidated, and with the bumper harvest of agricultural products, smuggling has been suppressed, financial stability, and the start of income tax collection, the central government's finances will definitely tend to balance with a little time. (See September 7th Current Affairs News) This conversation clearly revealed that the future of the central government's finances seems very promising. As a result, the general optimists feel that their theory is a manifestation of the facts. However, the previous reports of improved finances are still only verbal hearsay. Therefore, whether China's finances have improved or deteriorated cannot but depend on the facts in the next six months of the appointment period to explain. However, everything among human beings is governed by the law of cause and effect. Although we cannot make a definite assertion about future facts like a prophet, we can more or less infer some things from the past cause. Whether the inference is wrong or not depends on the future facts to compare.

Here, we will begin to infer the future of China's finances and review the two different theories about China's finances.

Speaking of the most obvious crisis in China's finances in recent years, everyone will point out the phenomenon of unbalanced revenue and expenditure. According to the government's publicly announced figures, since 1928, the annual revenue shortfall has often been around 100 million yuan. Among the years with final accounts (from 1928 to 1934), the largest deficit was 147 million yuan in 1933, accounting for 19.2% of the expenditure. Although there are no official final account figures for the two years after 1934 and 1935, the shortfall is still over 100 million yuan. Although this kind of financial imbalance is a modern, worldwide epidemic, it seems unremarkable, but for China's poor and weak national economy, its severity cannot be compared with other countries. In the past decade, the annual deficit of more than 100 million yuan has been almost entirely made up for by public debt policies. This public debt policy, until the forced exchange of unified public debt in February of this year, has felt that its future hope has been reduced. (According to the facts, since July 1935, the monthly fund for the repayment of domestic debt has been less than 4 million yuan.) Taking a step back, even if the public debt policy still has digestive power in today's China, but that year-after-year imbalance will eventually hit a wall. Therefore, at present, everyone feels that the adjustment of China's finances should start with balancing revenue and expenditure first, so at the time of the currency system reform last year, the statement that revenue and expenditure could be balanced after 18 months was put forward, so that everyone could have a strong sympathy for the currency system reform.

Whether China's finances can really be balanced after 18 months of currency system reform, as I have said before, is still difficult to say, but judging from the current financial situation, the practice of this statement is by no means an easy task. The year 1935 has now passed, and we will not worry about it for the time being. If we study the budget for the fiscal year 1936, which began on July 1, we find that it is not only unbalanced in revenue and expenditure, but even its unbalanced figure has appeared a new record high. The total revenue and expenditure for the fiscal year 1936 were 990.7 million yuan (this is the highest amount since China has had a budget). Although it maintains a balance on the surface, in fact, if we carefully examine the content of the revenue, we know that more than 200 million yuan of this is borrowed money and fictitious income. We can list the non-tax revenue in the budget for the past two years as a decision table. (Unit: 1,000 yuan)

From this table, we can see how rapidly the non-tax revenue in China's finances has been advancing in recent years, but this figure is unbelievable. The easiest to see is the item of net profit of state-owned enterprises, which has actually increased from 8 million yuan to more than 40 million yuan in a very short period of one or two years (more than 5 times), which contains some exaggeration. (See later for details) In addition, like the two items of state-owned property income and miscellaneous revenue and expenditure, the figures for the fiscal year 1935 increased compared with the fiscal year 1934, but the figures for the fiscal year 1936 have decreased compared with the fiscal year 1935, which precisely indicates that too much was falsely listed in the past, and now we have to reduce it a little. On the whole, the non-tax revenues for the fiscal year 1936 are less than those for the previous year, but the total amount has increased by 40 million yuan compared with the previous year, which is because the item of loan revenue has increased by 55 million yuan. According to a certain statistic, the deficit of the central government's finances in the past year reached 170 million yuan. Then, we can infer that the deficit for the fiscal year 1936 should be more than 220 million yuan. (According to the report of Legislative Committee member Chen Changheng, the deficit is about 200 million yuan.) Those who are looking forward to the balance of fiscal revenue and expenditure in six months (18 months) may feel disappointed when they see such a large deficit that has never been seen before.

Current Commentary

The Significance of the US Presidential Election

— Star

The US presidential election will be held on the 4th of next month. For several days, the election campaign has reached a fever pitch. The Republican and Democratic parties are evenly matched. The outcome depends on the effectiveness of the propaganda in these few remaining days. According to Reuters, Roosevelt has gained an advantage in thirty-two states and could get 70% of the electoral votes. Landon (the Republican presidential candidate) has a slight victory in sixteen states and could get 30% of the electoral votes. However, according to the test of the New York literary and artistic weekly, the result is the opposite. Landon can win the advantage of thirty-two states, while Roosevelt has the hope of winning only sixteen states. The ratio of voting power is 370 to 161, which is a big difference. It is because in this election, there are quite a lot of voters in a state of hesitation. Larger states such as New York are admittedly undecided. However, unless there are special changes, Roosevelt's chances of winning seem to be greater than Landon's.

This election is of great significance. The impact of who wins or loses is not limited to the personal gains and losses of Roosevelt or Landon. As far as the future of the US national economy is concerned, Roosevelt advocates reform, with the state controlling the nation's economic activities, so that capitalism does not fall into anarchy and self-destruction. Landon advocates conservatism, wanting to restore the state before 1933, advocating individualism and free competition, and regarding state intervention in private economic activities as the beginning of dictatorship and autocracy. He also wants to balance the budget and reduce relief expenses. Therefore, if Landon wins, the United States will return to the old economic anarchy. Laborers, poor farmers, and the unemployed will inevitably feel pain. This is one aspect. In terms of the political future of the United States, Roosevelt advocates centralization, advocating the expansion of the powers granted to the federal government by the constitution, to meet the requirements of the times. If there are difficulties, he will not hesitate to amend the constitution and reduce the power of the Supreme Court. Landon advocates protecting the freedom of the people and the power of the states, and regards the constitution and the Supreme Court as sacred and inviolable. If he wins, the political institutions of the United States will not be able to cope with the current social and economic demands. This is the second aspect.

In terms of diplomacy, although both advocate a policy of international isolation and vigorously promote the maintenance of peace, their attitudes are quite different. Roosevelt said that arms merchants are the creators of war. To achieve neutrality, we must first guard against the profiteering of international bankers and international arms dealers. He also deeply feels that the increase in economic barriers is the cause of ill will between countries. To achieve peace, we must engage in negotiating reciprocal tariff treaties and seek international amity through economic cooperation. Therefore, Roosevelt's attitude is self-critical and constructive. Landon is not like that. He vigorously opposes the League of Nations and the World Court, advocates expanding the army, navy, and air force, avoiding cooperation with other countries, canceling reciprocal tariff agreements, and wants to recover war debts and urge other countries to disarm. His attitude is accusatory and passive. In the days when Roosevelt is in power, the League of Nations and peace-loving countries still have the possibility of working hand in hand with Washington. If Landon is elected, narrow nationalism will dominate Washington's foreign policy, and the hope of international cooperation will be even more remote.

Now, in Europe and the Far East, the terror of war has reached its peak. Whether the destruction of human civilization can be postponed to after 1936 is quite a question. The war in Spain has put the Soviet Union and Germany and Italy in a state of enemies. Japan's active actions against China put the peace in the Far East in a precarious situation. The United States is the world's largest peaceful force, and its national destiny is closely related to the peace in any corner of the world. Recently, the direct Pacific air route between China and the United States has been opened, and Mr. He Huai De, a leader of the press in that country, has also come eastward on the wind. It can be seen that the relationship between the Far East and the United States is becoming increasingly close. We should pay close attention to the change of the US head of state, and the people of that country should have a deeper understanding of the internal and external relations of China and other countries in the world. Empty talk of isolation and avoiding cooperation may not be the best plan. On the eve of the US general election, we wish the people of that country to have a realistic consideration.

The United States, because of a special treaty, should still enjoy the same rights and should be treated as an exception. 50th Anniversary of the Completion of the Statue of Liberty in the United States; Grand Celebrations in New York; US and French Flags Shine Together; Aircraft Soar in the Sky and Warships Fire Salutes

Roosevelt Reaffirms the Concept of Freedom and Peace

(New York) The Statue of Liberty on Bedloe's Island in New York Harbor was made by several famous French sculptors and is one of the great buildings in the United States. Since its unveiling on October 28, 1886, today marks its 50th anniversary. The US government held a celebration ceremony, and the scene was extremely grand. The statue itself is extremely magnificent (89 feet high, with a base area of 62 square feet and weighing 225 tons). Now decorated with the national flags of the United States and France, it is even more magnificent. Countless people gathered around the statue, and three warships and countless cruise ships were anchored in the harbor, all flying flags and streamers, traveling back and forth, adding to the joyful atmosphere. When President Roosevelt arrived on a ferry, the warships immediately fired a 21-gun salute, and a squadron of aircraft soared in the sky. Suddenly, naval warships and merchant ships, aircraft and seaplanes in the air, all paraded in front of President Roosevelt, Mayor LaGuardia of New York City, the French government representative, namely Tedson, Assistant to the French State Council, the French Ambassador to the United States, De La Perre, and the US Secretary of the Interior, Ikes. All the dignitaries made speeches. President Roosevelt's speech said, "Those who presented the statue earlier had the same desire as our country, that is, freedom and peace are one. My belief is nothing else, that modern civilization will be improved." At the same time, French President Lebrun also delivered a broadcast speech from Paris to the United States, stating that the friendship between France and the United States has the power to last forever, and can be seen at this grand event. "Freedom is the main condition for progress, it was so in the past, and it is still so today," he said. (28th, Havas)

US General Election; Date Approaching

Voter Registration Breaks Records

(New York) The date of the US presidential election is less than a week away, so the presidential candidates of all parties are making every effort to win the final victory. Roosevelt and Landon both arrived in New York at the same time after traveling across the country. President Luo had taken a short rest in Washington to prepare for his final speech, so he did not look dusty. When he arrived in New York, the welcoming crowd was very crowded. Mr. Landon arrived in New York after Mr. Luo, and the grand welcome was the same. When Luo and Lan entered the city of New York, the New York police authorities dispatched about 3,000 policemen to guard the route. The first thing President Luo did after arriving in New York was to preside over the 50th anniversary celebration of the founding of the Statue of Liberty and give a speech, saying, "Even in the turbulent times at the moment, I still believe that a better civilization than we have known will appear in America, or it may be extended to the world." Roosevelt also said that this Statue of Liberty, in addition to symbolizing freedom, should be promoted and broadened to make it a symbol of peace. At the same time, people across the country have speculated a lot about the results of the general election next Tuesday. The US Postmaster and Roosevelt's campaign manager, Mr. Fa Lei, predicted that Luo would win an absolute victory. At the same time, Republican Chairman Hamilton also believed that Landon would defeat Roosevelt. The current number of registered voters across the country has reached 55,427,000, an increase of 15,000,000 from 1932, breaking the previous record. (28th, Reuters)

British Press Giants Point Out Weaknesses

British policy is uncertain, and the Singapore naval base is one example. Originally, it was intended to make it a British fortress in the Far East, but now it is of no value for large-scale wars. The Non-Intervention Committee; No Results in the Dispute; Soviet Russia's Attitude Remains Unclear; Britain, Germany, and Italy Favor Portugal and Suppress Russia

(London) Fearing that the governments of Soviet Russia and Portugal would not attend the Adjustment Committee on Non-Intervention in the Spanish Civil War, the representatives of the two countries still attended the meeting today, which lasted for six hours, focusing on considering Soviet Russia's accusations against Portugal for violating the non-intervention agreement, and Portugal's counter-accusations against Soviet Russia for interfering in Spanish affairs and promoting the civil war in the country. Soviet Russia mentioned a letter of explanation in response to recent Portuguese counter-accusations, saying that Soviet Russia was prepared to discuss the suggestions put forward by Committee Chairman Woon Lai Mao Zi to control the ports of the two countries and the Spanish border, and that if the legitimate government of Spain agreed, Soviet Russia would not oppose the implementation of control in the Spanish seaports and border areas not occupied by the rebel army. Soviet Russia asked the committee to immediately begin discussing this proposal.

The Portuguese representative did not accept the Soviet Russian proposal to control Portuguese ports. Chairman Pride Mouth explained that the British government was only concerned about suggestions to prevent the Spanish war from becoming an international war. Italian representative Grandi pointed out that Soviet Russia's remarks were ambiguous, saying that Soviet Russia's attitude really shocked the newspapers and encouraged one side of the war to prolong the war. Then Soviet Russian representative Mesky rose and said that Soviet Russia really wanted to combine the suggestion to control Portuguese ports with the suggestion put forward by Pride Mouth later to control Spanish ports and coastal areas. The Portuguese representative also accused Soviet Russia of being erratic, saying that it was difficult to discuss Portugal's accusations before the Soviet Russian representative. He regarded the ambassador's attendance as sufficient to indicate that Soviet Russia was still bound by the non-intervention agreement. Then Grandi, representing the Italian government, firmly denied the accusations against Italy. The Soviet Russian representative replied that the Italian statement was as unsatisfactory as the German reply. Mr. Mei also said that the Italian government continued to violate the non-intervention agreement in Spain and Mada. Then the chairman officially said that after a thorough investigation of the accusations against Italy, it was known that there was no real evidence. The accusations either occurred before Italy joined the agreement or never occurred. French representative Corban stated that the French government supports the entire non-intervention agreement and intends to make every effort to make the agreement effective. The French government is prepared to study any practical plan to control seaports and intends to participate in any plan that other governments have agreed to. Then the chairman stated that Soviet Russia's position was still unclear and asked whether Soviet Russia was still bound by the non-intervention agreement or had withdrawn from the obligations of the non-intervention agreement. Wei Nai announced that the subcommittee would reconvene on November 2, and the General Committee would convene on November 4. (28th, Reuters)

The Truth About Italian-German Talks; Seeking to Win Over Britain; Hope for Compromise on the Locarno Issue

(Rome) Regarding the results of Foreign Minister Ciano's visit to Germany, there is much speculation from the outside world, or that Italy will "distance itself" from the League of Nations. According to reliable sources in diplomatic circles here, Germany now wants to be close to Britain. It is generally believed here that this is an extension of the joint Italian-German front. Therefore, the rumors from the outside world that Italy and the government must require Britain to first explain its policies in the Mediterranean before proceeding with talks with it have become a non-issue. This can be seen from the fact that the Italian newspapers were detained by the government for any content that was unfavorable to Britain when Count Ciano visited Berlin a few days ago. In addition, when General Miller, director of the German Aviation Department, visited Rome a few days ago, he was heard to have proposed a Locarno Pact in the sky to General Valey, director of the Italian Aviation Department, and asked Britain to participate together (France will wait for Britain to participate before inviting it to join). This is also enough to prove that Italy wants to be close to Britain. As for the negotiations between Britain and Italy on the issue of convening a Locarno Conference, which have been delayed for a long time, there is now hope for a compromise. (29th, Havas)

Romania and Czechoslovakia Decide to Cooperate with Germany and Italy to Resolve Central European Issues; Romania's Neutrality Movement Expands

Prague, Czechoslovakia – King Carol II of Romania arrived here this morning and met with Czech Prime Minister Hodza. Foreign Minister Crovda then visited President Beneš. King Carol, Foreign Minister Antonescu, President Beneš, and Foreign Minister Crovda held a meeting to discuss the international situation. Afterward, a communiqué was issued stating that the Romanian and Czech authorities had reached a consensus. It also stated that the Little Entente countries are willing to sincerely cooperate with the signatories of the Rome Protocols (Italy, Austria, and Hungary) and Germany on various European issues. Furthermore, the resolution adopted at the recent standing political conference of the Little Entente countries held in Bratislava, Czechoslovakia, namely "The Little Entente countries do not interfere in the internal affairs of other countries, but other countries must not interfere in the internal affairs of the Little Entente countries," is hereby reaffirmed and will be implemented. President Beneš hosted a banquet in the evening to welcome the Romanian King. During the banquet, the leaders of both countries delivered speeches emphasizing the unity of the Little Entente countries, which remains unchanged from the past. (Havas News Agency, 28th)

Bucharest, Romania – A movement advocating a neutral policy has recently emerged in the country and is gaining momentum. Its arguments are based on two points: (1) collective security mechanisms have failed, and (2) the public harbors antipathy towards the Soviet Union. It is also argued that a conflict between Russia and Germany is likely, and if Romania does not wish to be drawn into the vortex, it must unite the Baltic states, the Little Entente countries, the Balkan Entente countries, and Poland to form a strong neutral bloc to maintain armed neutrality. This movement is led by Brătianu, a leader of the Liberal Party's splinter faction, and is supported by the extreme right and a portion of the right wing. However, the majority of the Liberal Party members, the Peasants' Party, and the Conservative Party have expressed opposition. They believe that this is an attempt by Germany to exploit the Little Entente countries' interconnected relationships to undermine the mutual assistance pact between Russia and Czechoslovakia. These individuals have expressed their delight at King Carol II's visit to Czechoslovakia, believing that the outcome of this trip will ensure that Romania's alliance system within the framework of the League of Nations will be fully maintained. (Havas News Agency, 29th)

French Finance Minister Explains New Budget

Deficit of Six Billion Francs; Plans to Find New Ways to Restore Balance

(Paris) French Finance Minister Olivol appeared before the Finance Committee of the Chamber of Deputies this afternoon to explain the main points of the 1937 budget. The budget is scheduled to be submitted to the Chamber of Deputies for discussion at the end of next month. Olivol first discussed the financial situation in 1936, stating that despite the government's efforts to economize, the actual financial deficit reached a staggering 6,000,000,000 francs due to various unexpected expenditures. The total expenditure for this year is approximately 50,000,000,000 francs, which is not much different from that of 1933. As long as the international situation does not ease and financial market interest rates do not decrease, expenditure on national defense and debt will not be reduced. Previous governments sought to make up for the financial deficit by reducing public works, saving wages and salaries, and increasing taxes. The current government plans to find new ways to restore budget balance. (Havas News Agency, 28th)

(Paris) After the Finance Minister explained the content of the new budget to the Finance Committee of the Chamber of Deputies yesterday, it has been learned that the temporary expenditure section of the budget includes 8,500,000,000 francs for national defense and 3,500,000,000 francs for public works, totaling 12,000,000,000 francs. These will be financed by issuing special government bonds. Added to the regular expenditure of 47,000,000,000 francs, the total amounts to 59,000,000,000 francs. Regarding revenue, in addition to reducing various indirect taxes and increasing income taxes, the tax rate on large inheritances will also be increased, while the tax rate on small inheritances will be reduced. Furthermore, the government plans to improve various public utilities to simplify them and save expenses. (Havas News Agency, 29th)
